Your job is to implement a full ASP.NET Core MVC\nweb application for a metal music quiz — a daily \"guess the song\" experience\nsimilar to Songdle. The app uses mock repositories with static data (no real\ndatabase). All code must follow ASP.NET MVC conventions with Razor views,\nproper routing, dependency injection, and a unique non-standard UX/UI.\n\n---\n\n## STEP 0 — BEFORE WRITING ANY UI CODE: SPAWN THE UX SUB-AGENT\n\nBefore generating any .cshtml view, layout, or CSS file, you MUST invoke the\nUX sub-agent. Log the following to the console output AND append it to a file called\n   `logs/ux-agent-calls.log`:\n   ```\n   [UX-AGENT INVOKED] Timestamp: <current datetime>\n   Task: <brief description of the UI being generated>\n   Instructions source: .agents/ux-agent-instructions.md\n   ```\n\n3. Apply the UX agent's style rules to every view you generate.\n\nThis log is required as proof of sub-agent usage. You are invoked by the main coding agent\nbefore any UI code is written.\n\n## Theme & Aesthetic\n- Dark, high-contrast theme: black/near-black backgrounds (#0a0a0a, #111111)\n- Accent colors: blood red (#8b0000 / #cc0000) and bone white (#e8e0d0)\n- Secondary accent: rusted gold (#b8860b) for highlights and badges\n- Typography: use Google Fonts — \"Metal Mania\" for headings, \"Share Tech Mono\"\n  for body/data text (monospace feel, like a terminal/setlist)\n- Texture: subtle noise/grain CSS filter on the body background\n- NO default Bootstrap navbar or card styles — override everything\n\n## Layout Principles\n- Fixed left-side vertical navigation panel (width: 220px) with band logo /\n  app title at top, nav links below, and a small \"daily streak\" counter\n  at the bottom\n- Main content area fills the remaining width with a max-width of 1100px\n- Breadcrumbs rendered as a minimal slash-separated line above page titles:\n  e.g.  Home / Bands / Metallica\n- Page titles use large, uppercase, letter-spaced headings with a thin red\n  left-border accent\n- Avoid centered layouts — align content left/grid-based\n\n## Component Style Rules\n- Tables: no default borders; use alternating row backgrounds (#111 / #1a1a1a),\n  red left-border on hover, monospace text\n- Cards (for Details pages): dark bordered panels, red top-accent stripe,\n  label-value pairs in a two-column definition list style\n- Buttons: flat, rectangular, uppercase, red background with white text —\n  NO rounded corners, NO box-shadows\n- Links: bone white by default, red on hover, NO underline\n- Badges/tags (e.g. genre tags): small pill-shaped, dark red background,\n  bone white text\n\n## Navigation\n- Left sidebar contains links to: Home (Daily Quiz), Bands, Albums, Songs,\n  Genres\n- Active link is highlighted with a red left-border and slightly lighter bg\n- Breadcrumbs appear on every page except Home\n\n## Custom Home Page (Songdle-style Daily Quiz)\n- Full-height hero panel with the question: \"Guess today's metal song\"\n- Show a waveform placeholder or album art placeholder (blurred/hidden)\n- Reveal clues one by one (band initials → album year → genre → first lyric)\n- A text input + submit button for the user's guess\n- A result panel that shows: correct answer, album cover, band info, and a\n  link to that song's Details page\n- Show a daily streak counter and a share button (static, no backend needed)\n\n## Spacing & Sizing\n- Base spacing unit: 8px\n- Section padding: 24px\n- Sidebar item height: 48px\n- Font sizes: headings 2rem–3rem, body 0.95rem, labels 0.75rem uppercase\n\n## Do NOT Use\n- Default Bootstrap navbar, jumbotron, or card classes\n- Any pastel or light color schemes\n- Centered hero text layouts typical of generic Bootstrap templates\n```\n```\n\n---\n\n## STEP 2 — PROJECT STRUCTURE\n\nEnsure the ASP.NET Core MVC project has the following structure:\n\n```\n/Controllers\n    HomeController.cs         ← Daily Quiz (custom home page)\n    BandController.cs\n    AlbumController.cs\n    SongController.cs\n    GenreController.cs\n\n/Models\n    /Domain\n        Band.cs\n        Album.cs\n        Song.cs\n        Genre.cs\n    /Mock\n        BandMockRepository.cs\n        AlbumMockRepository.cs\n        SongMockRepository.cs\n        GenreMockRepository.cs\n    /ViewModels\n        BandIndexViewModel.cs\n        BandDetailsViewModel.cs\n        AlbumIndexViewModel.cs\n        AlbumDetailsViewModel.cs\n        SongIndexViewModel.cs\n        SongDetailsViewModel.cs\n        GenreIndexViewModel.cs\n        GenreDetailsViewModel.cs\n        DailyQuizViewModel.cs\n\n/Views\n    /Home\n        Index.cshtml            ← Songdle-style daily quiz page\n    /Band\n        Index.cshtml\n        Details.cshtml\n    /Album\n        Index.cshtml\n        Details.cshtml\n    /Song\n        Index.cshtml\n        Details.cshtml\n    /Genre\n        Index.cshtml\n        Details.cshtml\n    /Shared\n        _Layout.cshtml\n        _Breadcrumbs.cshtml     ← partial view\n\n/wwwroot\n    /css\n        site.css                ← all custom UX agent styles\n\n/.agents\n    ux-agent-instructions.md\n\n/logs\n    ux-agent-calls.log\n\nProgram.cs\n```\n\n---\n\n## STEP 3 — DOMAIN MODEL\n\nCreate the following C# domain model classes. Use static data\n(at least 6 bands, 3 albums per band, 4 songs per album, 5 genres):\n\n```csharp\n// Genre.cs\npublic class Genre {\n    public int Id { get; set; }\n    public string Name { get; set; }          // e.g. \"Thrash Metal\"\n    public string Description { get; set; }\n}\n\n// Band.cs\npublic class Band {\n    public int Id { get; set; }\n    public string Name { get; set; }\n    public int FormedYear { get; set; }\n    public string Country { get; set; }\n    public Genre Genre { get; set; }\n    public string Description { get; set; }\n    public List<Album> Albums { get; set; }\n}\n\n// Album.cs\npublic class Album {\n    public int Id { get; set; }\n    public string Title { get; set; }\n    public int ReleaseYear { get; set; }\n    public Band Band { get; set; }\n    public List<Song> Songs { get; set; }\n}\n\n// Song.cs\npublic class Song {\n    public int Id { get; set; }\n    public string Title { get; set; }\n    public int DurationSeconds { get; set; }\n    public Album Album { get; set; }\n    public string OpeningLyric { get; set; }   // used as clue in quiz\n    public bool IsDailyQuizSong { get; set; }  // one song marked true\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## STEP 4 — MOCK REPOSITORIES\n\nEach repository must be registered as a Singleton in Program.cs.\nEach must implement at minimum:\n- `GetAll()` — returns full list\n- `GetById(int id)` — returns single item or null\n\nExample registration in Program.cs:\n```csharp\nbuilder.Services.AddSingleton<BandMockRepository>();\nbuilder.Services.AddSingleton<AlbumMockRepository>();\nbuilder.Services.AddSingleton<SongMockRepository>();\nbuilder.Services.AddSingleton<GenreMockRepository>();\n```\n\nPopulate each repository with realistic metal music static data inline\n(do not read from files or databases).\n\n---\n\n## STEP 5 — CONTROLLERS\n\nEach controller receives its repository via constructor injection.\nImplement ONLY the following actions (no Create/Edit/Delete):\n\n### BandController\n- `Index()` → passes List<Band> to view\n- `Details(int id)` → passes single Band (with albums) to view\n\n### AlbumController\n- `Index()` → passes List<Album> to view\n- `Details(int id)` → passes single Album (with songs and band) to view\n\n### SongController\n- `Index()` → passes List<Song> to view\n- `Details(int id)` → passes single Song (with album and band) to view\n\n### GenreController\n- `Index()` → passes List<Genre> to view\n- `Details(int id)` → passes Genre + all bands in that genre to view\n\n### HomeController\n- `Index()` → find the Song where IsDailyQuizSong == true, build\n  DailyQuizViewModel, pass to view\n- `[HttpPost] Index(string guess)` → compare guess to daily song title\n  (case-insensitive), set result in ViewModel, return view\n\n---\n\n## STEP 6 — VIEWS\n\n### _Layout.cshtml\n- Implement the left sidebar navigation per UX agent rules\n- Include Google Fonts links for \"Metal Mania\" and \"Share Tech Mono\"\n- RenderBody() in the main content area\n- RenderSection(\"Breadcrumbs\", required: false) just below the sidebar\n\n### _Breadcrumbs.cshtml (partial)\n- Accepts a list of (Label, Url) tuples via ViewData[\"Breadcrumbs\"]\n- Renders as:  Home / Bands / Metallica  with clickable links\n\n### Index views (Band, Album, Song, Genre)\n- Render a styled table (per UX agent table rules)\n- Each row has a \"View Details\" link using asp-controller / asp-action /\n  asp-route-id tag helpers\n- Include breadcrumbs\n\n### Details views\n- Use a card/panel layout (per UX agent card rules)\n- Show all relevant fields\n- Band Details: list albums as a mini-table with links to Album Details\n- Album Details: list songs as a mini-table with links to Song Details\n- Song Details: show album and band with navigation links\n- Genre Details: list all bands in that genre with links\n- All Details pages have a \"← Back to list\" link\n- Include breadcrumbs\n\n### Home/Index.cshtml (Daily Quiz — Songdle style)\n- Per UX agent custom home page spec\n- Show clues progressively using @if blocks based on attempt count\n  stored in ViewData or ViewModel\n- The guess form POSTs to Home/Index\n- Show result panel if ViewModel.IsAnswered == true\n\n---\n\n## STEP 7 — ROUTING\n\nUse the default route pattern in Program.cs:\n```csharp\napp.MapControllerRoute(\n    name: \"default\",\n    pattern: \"{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}\");\n```\n\nAll navigation must use asp-* tag helpers (not hardcoded href strings).\n\n---\n\n## STEP 8 — CSS (wwwroot/css/site.css)\n\nImplement all styles defined in the UX agent instruction file.\nDo NOT rely on default Bootstrap styles for layout or components —\noverride or replace them entirely. Bootstrap may still be loaded for\nits reset/grid base only.\n\n---\n\n## STEP 9 — GIT\n\nAfter completing all steps, ensure the following are committed to the\ndefault branch:\n- All source code\n- `.agents/ux-agent-instructions.md`\n- `logs/ux-agent-calls.log` (with at least one logged UX agent call entry)\n\nCommit message suggestion:\n`feat: Lab 2 - HTML/Binding - Metal quiz MVC app with UX sub-agent`\n\n---\n\n## CONSTRAINTS & REMINDERS\n\n- NO Create / Edit / Delete pages or actions\n- NO real database — mock repositories only\n- NO default Bootstrap navbar or card visual styles\n- UX agent MUST be logged before any view is written\n- All links between pages must work (list → details → back)\n- Breadcrumbs must appear on every page except the Home/quiz page\n- Be ready to explain: controller → repository → viewmodel → view data flow,\n  how routing resolves URLs, and how the UX sub-agent pattern works\n```\n\n---\n\n## How to use this\n\n1.
